   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    2009 in film
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
    </div>
    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
     Jump to:
     <a href="#mw-head">
      navigation
     </a>
     ,
     <a href="#p-search">
      search
     </a>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <p>
      The year 2009 saw the release of many films. Seven made the
      <a href="/wiki/List_of_highest-grossing_films" title="List of highest-grossing films">
       top 50 list of highest-grossing films
      </a>
      . Also in 2009, the
      <a href="/wiki/Academy_of_Motion_Picture_Arts_and_Sciences" title="Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences">
       Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences
      </a>
      announced that as of that year, their Best Picture category would consist of ten nominees, rather than five (the first time since the 1943 awards).
     </p>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Events">
       Events
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=2009_in_film&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Events">

       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <table>
      <tr>
       <td>
        January
       </td>
       <td>
        <i>
         22
        </i>
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/81st_Academy_Awards" title="81st Academy Awards">
         81st
         <b>
          Academy Awards
         </b>
        </a>
        nominations are announced with
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/The_Curious_Case_of_Benjamin_Button_(film)" title="The Curious Case of Benjamin Button (film)">
          The Curious Case of Benjamin Button
         </a>
        </i>
        leading with 13 nominations, followed by
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Slumdog_Millionaire" title="Slumdog Millionaire">
          Slumdog Millionaire
         </a>
        </i>
        with 10. Both films are nominated for
        <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Picture" title="Academy Award for Best Picture">
         Best Picture
        </a>
        .
        <a href="/wiki/Heath_Ledger" title="Heath Ledger">
         Heath Ledger
        </a>
        is
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Posthumous_recognition" title="Posthumous recognition">
         posthumously
        </a>
        nominated for
        <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Supporting_Actor" title="Academy Award for Best Supporting Actor">
         Best Supporting Actor award
        </a>
        for his performance in
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/The_Dark_Knight_(film)" title="The Dark Knight (film)">
          The Dark Knight
         </a>
        </i>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
       </td>
       <td>
        <i>
         25
        </i>
       </td>
       <td>
        The 15th
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Screen_Actors_Guild_Awards" title="Screen Actors Guild Awards">
         Screen Actors Guild Awards
        </a>
        ceremony is held at the Shrine Exposition Center, Los Angeles.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
       </td>
       <td>
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/36th_Annie_Awards" title="36th Annie Awards">
         Annie Awards
        </a>
        ceremony is held in the UCLA's Royce Hall, Los Angeles.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
       </td>
       <td>
        <i>
         31
        </i>
       </td>
       <td>

        <a href="/wiki/Directors_Guild_of_America_Award" title="Directors Guild of America Award">

        </a>
        dinner is held in the Hyatt Regency Century Plaza, Los Angeles.

       </td>
       <td>

        </i>
       </td>
       <td>
        The 59th
        <a href="/wiki/Berlin_International_Film_Festival" title="Berlin International Film Festival">
         Berlin International Film Festival
        </a>
        is opened with the world premiere of
        <a href="/wiki/Tom_Tykwer" title="Tom Tykwer">
         Tom Tykwer
        </a>
        's
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/The_International_(2009_film)" title="The International (2009 film)">
          The International
         </a>
        </i>
        . The
        <b>
         Golden Bear
        </b>
        prize is awarded to
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/The_Milk_of_Sorrow" title="The Milk of Sorrow">
          The Milk of Sorrow
         </a>
        </i>
        . The
        <b>
         Silver Bear
        </b>
        s prizes are awarded to
        <a href="/wiki/Asghar_Farhadi" title="Asghar Farhadi">
         Asghar Farhadi
        </a>
        ,
        <i>
         Best Director
        </i>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Sotigui_Kouyat%C3%A9" title="Sotigui Kouyat">
         Sotigui Kouyat
        </a>
        ,
        <i>
         Best Actor
        </i>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Birgit_Minichmayr" title="Birgit Minichmayr">
         Birgit Minichmayr
        </a>
        ,
        <i>
         Best Actress
        </i>
        . The festival is closed by the international premiere of
        <a href="/wiki/George_Tillman,_Jr." title="George Tillman, Jr.">
         George Tillman, Jr.
        </a>
        's
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Notorious_(2009_film)" title="Notorious (2009 film)">
          Notorious
         </a>
        </i>
       </td>
      </tr>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Events_2">
       Events
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>

     <table>
      <tr>
       <td>
        January
       </td>
       <td>
        <i>
         22
        </i>
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/81st_Academy_Awards" title="81st Academy Awards">
         81st
         <b>
          Academy Awards
         </b>
        </a>
        nominations are announced with
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/The_Curious_Case_of_Benjamin_Button_(film)" title="The Curious Case of Benjamin Button (film)">
          The Curious Case of Benjamin Button
         </a>
        </i>
        leading with 13 nominations, followed by
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Slumdog_Millionaire" title="Slumdog Millionaire">
          Slumdog Millionaire
         </a>
        </i>
        with 10. Both films are nominated for
        <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Picture" title="Academy Award for Best Picture">
         Best Picture
        </a>
        .
        <a href="/wiki/Heath_Ledger" title="Heath Ledger">
         Heath Ledger
        </a>
        is
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Posthumous_recognition" title="Posthumous recognition">
         posthumously
        </a>
        nominated for
        <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Supporting_Actor" title="Academy Award for Best Supporting Actor">
         Best Supporting Actor award
        </a>
        for his performance in
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/The_Dark_Knight_(film)" title="The Dark Knight (film)">
          The Dark Knight
         </a>
        </i>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>

        </a>
        ceremony is held at the Shrine Exposition Center, Los Angeles.

         </a>
        </i>
        . The
        <b>

        </a>

        <i>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2009_films">
       2009 films
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=2009_in_film&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2009 films">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Films released in North America in 2009 include:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       W: wide release (600 or more theaters)
      </li>
      <li>
       L: limited release in select cities (fewer than 600 theaters)
      </li>
      <li>
       R: re-release of previously released film
      </li>
      <li>
       : films that achieved wide-release status after initial release
      </li>
     </ul>
